    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',

<span id="freeTextContainer8290926401508684610"><b>Twin sisters separated by the past are reunited by unspeakable crimes in <i>New York Times</i> bestselling author Mary Burton’s throat-clutching novel of suspense…</b><br/><br/>Trauma victims are not new to medical examiner Faith McIntyre, but this one is different.   <span id="freeText8290926401508684610" style="display:none"><b>Twin sisters separated by the past are reunited by unspeakable crimes in <i>New York Times</i> bestselling author Mary Burton’s throat-clutching novel of suspense…</b><br /><br />Trauma victims are not new to medical examiner Faith McIntyre, but this one is different. The unconscious woman clinging to life after a hit and run is FBI agent Macy Crow. What the woman from Quantico was doing in a dark alley after midnight is just one mystery. The other is more unsettling: Macy is Faith’s mirror image—the twin sister she never knew she had.<br /><br />Faith knew that she was adopted, but now she’s finding that her childhood concealed other secrets. Following the trail of clues Macy left behind, Faith and Texas Ranger Mitchell Hayden make a shocking discovery on an isolated country ranch—a burial ground for three women who disappeared thirty years before.<br /><br />They weren’t the only victims in a killer’s twisted plot. And they won’t be the last.<br /><br />As the missing pieces of Faith’s and Macy’s dark lives snap into place, Faith is becoming more terrified by what she sees—and by what she must do to save her sister and herself from the past.</span>
  <a data-text-id="8290926401508684610" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          $$('div.prototip').each(function(i){i.setStyle({zIndex: 6000})});
        }
      });

      newTip['wrapper'].addClassName('prototipAllowOverflow');

        $('edition_39344119').observe('prototip:shown', function () {
          $$('div.prototip').each(function (e) {
            if ($('edition_39344119').hasClassName('ignored')) {
              e.setStyle({'display': 'none'});
              return;
            }
            e.setStyle({'overflow': 'visible'});
          });
        });
      $('edition_39344119').observe('prototip:hidden', function () {
        $$('span.elementTwo').each(function (e) {
          if (e.getStyle('display') !== 'none') {
            var lessLink = e.next();
            swapContent(lessLink);
          }
        });
      });

//]]>
</script></div>
</li>

<div id="review_2503542780" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2503542780" />
    <a title="Carrie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/36817401-carrie"><img alt="Carrie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1415677371p2/36817401.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2503542780?book_show_action=true">Oct 06, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Carrie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Carrie" href="/user/show/36817401-carrie">Carrie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/36817401-carrie?shelf=netgalley">netgalley</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2503542780" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7175371684420434865">Anyone who has picked up a novel by Mary Burton knows she does romantic suspense and does it very well and Cut and Run is no exception. This novel is a bit more on the thriller side than the romance but there’s still that relationship between the characters that fans want to see.<br/><br/>When a body of a man is found Faith McIntyre is the active medical examiner on the case and after her examination she tries to make contact with the victim’s daughter, Macy Crow. What Faith doesn’t know is that Macy does</span>
  <span id="freeText7175371684420434865" style="display:none">Anyone who has picked up a novel by Mary Burton knows she does romantic suspense and does it very well and Cut and Run is no exception. This novel is a bit more on the thriller side than the romance but there’s still that relationship between the characters that fans want to see.<br /><br />When a body of a man is found Faith McIntyre is the active medical examiner on the case and after her examination she tries to make contact with the victim’s daughter, Macy Crow. What Faith doesn’t know is that Macy does make her way to town and begins looking into her father’s murder herself being an FBI agent.<br /><br />Macy however makes the mistake of catching the attention of the wrong person and is run down by a truck. Texas Ranger Mitchell Hayden shows up at the scene of the accident to find the injured woman looks exactly like Faith whom he has been seeing. This leads Faith and Hayden to begin looking further into the case.<br /><br />Cut and Run of course is one that changes the point of view along the way mostly being the two main characters but also a few other views mixed in. The story however is one that is easy to follow as secrets of the past came hauntingly back to mix in with the intensity of the current time. Some may want to see a bit more romance but I rather enjoyed this one for the thrilling ride that is was and would definitely recommend checking it out.<br /><br />I received an advance copy from the publisher via Netgalley.<br /><br />For more reviews please visit <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://carriesbookreviews.com/">https://carriesbookreviews.com/</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="7175371684420434865" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_2554922512" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2554922512" />
    <a title="Carole (Carole&#39;s Random Life in Books)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5892196-carole-carole-s-random-life-in-books"><img alt="Carole (Carole&#39;s Random Life in Books)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1415550632p2/5892196.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2554922512?book_show_action=true">Oct 19, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Carole (Carole&#39;s Random Life in Books)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Carole (Carole&#39;s Random Life in Books)" href="/user/show/5892196-carole-carole-s-random-life-in-books">Carole (Carole&#39;s Random Life in Books)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5892196-carole-carole-s-random-life-in-books?shelf=mystery">mystery</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5892196-carole-carole-s-random-life-in-books?shelf=audio-book">audio-book</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5892196-carole-carole-s-random-life-in-books?shelf=2018">2018</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5892196-carole-carole-s-random-life-in-books?shelf=reviewed">reviewed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5892196-carole-carole-s-random-life-in-books?shelf=thriller">thriller</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5892196-carole-carole-s-random-life-in-books?shelf=own-kindle-copy">own-kindle-copy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5892196-carole-carole-s-random-life-in-books?shelf=won">won</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5892196-carole-carole-s-random-life-in-books?shelf=kindle-unlimited">kindle-unlimited</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2554922512" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11917861999672683053">This review can also be found at <a href='https://carolesrandomlife.blogspot.com/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Carole's Random Life in Books</a>.<br/><br/>I liked this book. I found it to be a really well done romantic suspense novel. This is a stand-alone novel but I did find a connection to another one of her books, The Last Move, through the characters which I found interesting. I found this book to be easy to listen to for hours at a time as I worked to try to solve the mystery. I ended up have a great time with this story.<br/><br/>The action starts right away in this book with the discover</span>
  <span id="freeText11917861999672683053" style="display:none">This review can also be found at <a href="https://carolesrandomlife.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Carole's Random Life in Books</a>.<br /><br />I liked this book. I found it to be a really well done romantic suspense novel. This is a stand-alone novel but I did find a connection to another one of her books, The Last Move, through the characters which I found interesting. I found this book to be easy to listen to for hours at a time as I worked to try to solve the mystery. I ended up have a great time with this story.<br /><br />The action starts right away in this book with the discovery of the body of a man that has been tortured. This is just the start of a rather complicated and far-reaching chain of events. I really wasn't sure how everything would work out or how one thing was connected to the next but as the book progressed everything just seemed to fall into place. There are events from the past connected to other things that are happening in the present day which really added to the mystery.<br /><br />I liked the characters quite a bit. Faith is the medical examiner tasked with working on the initial body. She was smart and dedicated to the job. She was also the kind of person that really worked to help others and got personally involved at times. Macy is Faith's equal in every way and they share a much deeper connection. I wish that Macy could have been a bigger part of the story but I did appreciate what she did add to the tale. Ranger Hayden was good at his job and worked really well with Faith. They made a great team and it was fun to see all the pieces come together.<br /><br />I thought that Brittany Pressley did a great job with the story. This book had a rather large cast of characters and I thought she handled them all really well. She was able to add a lot of emotion to the story at times and was able to add some excitement to other scenes. This was my first time listening to Brittany Pressley's work but I was really impressed and hope to get the chance to listen to her narration again soon.<br /><br />I would recommend this book to fans of romantic suspense. I liked that the mystery element to this story seemed to take the main stage with the romance adding a nice extra element. I plan to read more from Mary Burton in the future.<br /><br /><i>I won a digital copy of this book in a Goodreads giveaway and borrowed the audio from Kindle Unlimited.</i><br /><br /><b>Initial Thoughts</b><br />I liked this one but not quite as much as I liked <i>The Last Move</i> by the same author. I was actually surprised to find that this book did have a small link to <i>The Last Move</i> through a character. Both books really are stand alones but the connection is there. Now I am wondering if there are other books that might have some kind of link. The story was pretty complex and spanned over 30 years. There were a few things that I was able to guess and some things that I couldn't. I did enjoy the story overall and thought that the narrator did a great job with the book.<br /><br />Book Source: I won an ebook copy through a Goodreads giveaway and borrowed a copy of the audiobook from Kindle Unlimited.</span>
  <a data-text-id="11917861999672683053" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_2540933934" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2540933934" />
    <a title=".Under the pages" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/40494464-under-the-pages"><img alt=".Under the pages" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1518366710p2/40494464.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">

<span id="freeTextContainer9982579242717772785"><b>NOW LIVE!</b><br/><a href='https://amzn.to/2xW68RB' rel='nofollow noopener'>Amazon US</a> * <a href='https://amzn.to/2Rlz1il' rel='nofollow noopener'>Amazon UK</a> <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1538588583ra/26396101.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Mary Burton's books just have everything I could ask for in a Romantic Suspense and this one was no different. With that little bit of romance between Faith and Mitchell, the on-the-edge-of-my-seat suspense, and the massive amount of intrigue, I was completely hooked on this story.   <span id="freeText9982579242717772785" style="display:none"><b>NOW LIVE!</b><br><a href="https://amzn.to/2xW68RB" rel="nofollow noopener">Amazon US</a> * <a href="https://amzn.to/2Rlz1il" rel="nofollow noopener">Amazon UK</a> <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1538588583ra/26396101.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Mary Burton's books just have everything I could ask for in a Romantic Suspense and this one was no different. With that little bit of romance between Faith and Mitchell, the on-the-edge-of-my-seat suspense, and the massive amount of intrigue, I was completely hooked on this story. It took me through twists and turns and had me guessing at everything. Even when I got to the point where I knew what was going on I still didn't actually know what was going to happen. I loved that it had me so shocked at multiple different times and each turn of the page had me wide eyed. <br><br>Overall, this is story-telling at it's finest. Ms. Burton will always be one of my favorite RS authors and each book I read from her only solidifies that fact. <br><br><i>ARC kindly provided in exchange for an honest review.</i></span>

<div id="review_2552653902" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2552653902" />
    <a title="Sheryl" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1771463-sheryl"><img alt="Sheryl" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1595720352p2/1771463.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2552653902?book_show_action=true">Oct 07, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sheryl" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sheryl" href="/user/show/1771463-sheryl">Sheryl</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1771463-sheryl?shelf=2018">2018</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1771463-sheryl?shelf=netgalley">netgalley</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1771463-sheryl?shelf=romantic-suspense">romantic-suspense</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2552653902" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10743487269374699481">What a fantastic read, this book has a little bit of everything but a lot of surprises that will keep guessing until the end.<br/>When Texas Ranger Mitchell Haydon receives a message from an old acquaintance, Jack Crow who has been known to live on the fringes of the law his interest is peaked. Unfortunately for Mr. Crow, he's a little late getting out to the Salvage yard where Crow lives. When Ranger Haydon arrives, let's just say he's chasing off the buzzards who are also interested in Mr. Crow. It</span>
  <span id="freeText10743487269374699481" style="display:none">What a fantastic read, this book has a little bit of everything but a lot of surprises that will keep guessing until the end.<br />When Texas Ranger Mitchell Haydon receives a message from an old acquaintance, Jack Crow who has been known to live on the fringes of the law his interest is peaked. Unfortunately for Mr. Crow, he's a little late getting out to the Salvage yard where Crow lives. When Ranger Haydon arrives, let's just say he's chasing off the buzzards who are also interested in Mr. Crow. It looks like ole Jack took whatever secrets that this killer wanted to the grave by the looks of his poor old tortured body and tossed trailer house. <br />Ranger Haydon calls in the reinforcements to see if they could come up with anything useful regarding who did this to the old man who was pretty much a hermit. <br />Medical Examiner Fatih McIntyre and her investigator arrive and take Mr. Crow away and look for the next of kin to identify the body. Mr. Crow had a son, Dirk who lived on the other side of the property who seems to be missing and a daughter Macy who lives in Virginia. They did make contact with Macy, and she drops everything and catches the next flight to Austin.<br />Macy’s first stop is her dad's salvage yard; she's sure that the two initial searches might have missed something. She's right, her dad left her trail, but it was in the right direction. She's back at her hotel room when she sees a clip Faith McIntyre accepting an award regarding a children's home. She's completely dumbfounded by the image Faith; it was like her body double. She sends Faith a note plus a selfie and photo of her FBI identification. <br /> She's following her trial to a bar called "Second Chances" when things go wrong. Macy is almost killed after she leaves that bar, Ranger Haydon can't believe what his eyes when approaches the body of Macy laying broken in the street. He's been working with Faith for a long time and knew she was an only child.<br /> As I stated earlier this book has so many twists and turns, I'm finding it hard to write this review without spewing spoilers all over the place. <br />Ms. Burton has done it again, another perfect romantic suspense novel that will rival anyone else's out there.<br />I would like to thank the publisher and NetGalley for providing me with a copy of this galley in exchange for my honest review. The opinions I expressed above are my own.</span>
  <a data-text-id="10743487269374699481" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2373041703" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2373041703" />
    <a title="Melanie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/23102950-melanie"><img alt="Melanie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1445470019p2/23102950.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2373041703?book_show_action=true">Oct 04, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Melanie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Melanie" href="/user/show/23102950-melanie">Melanie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781503902862" href="/book/show/39344107-cut-and-run">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/23102950-melanie?shelf=own-print">own-print</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/23102950-melanie?shelf=netgalley">netgalley</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/23102950-melanie?shelf=romantic-suspense">romantic-suspense</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2373041703" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6468578499595038697"><i>Cut and Run</i> was an incredibly enjoyable read with a fantastic suspense plot and an amazing set of characters.<br/><br/>Medical examiner Faith McIntyre is no stranger to death, but the torture and murder of Jack Crow feels different. After contacting his daughter FBI agent Macy Crow, Faith is awaiting the woman’s arrival when she receives word that Macy was the victim of a hit and run and is barely clinging to life in the hospital. The mystery of what she was doing in Austin after midnight is puzzling. Eve</span>
  <span id="freeText6468578499595038697" style="display:none"><i>Cut and Run</i> was an incredibly enjoyable read with a fantastic suspense plot and an amazing set of characters.<br /><br />Medical examiner Faith McIntyre is no stranger to death, but the torture and murder of Jack Crow feels different. After contacting his daughter FBI agent Macy Crow, Faith is awaiting the woman’s arrival when she receives word that Macy was the victim of a hit and run and is barely clinging to life in the hospital. The mystery of what she was doing in Austin after midnight is puzzling. Even more bizarre is the fact Macy is Faith’s mirror image, the twin sister she never knew she had. While following clues Macy left behind, three unmarked graves are discovered on an abandoned ranch containing the remains of women missing for thirty years. With bodies new and old piling up, it becomes clear someone is willing to kill to keep these secrets buried.<br /><br />Faith always knew she was adopted growing up but she hit roadblocks every time she tried to discover more information. While Faith is secure in who she is, she can’t help but wonder about her past. Faith devotes herself to helping kids without families and spends much of her time helping at a children’s shelter in town. Faith has formed a connection with one of the teenagers there Kat and I really enjoyed their relationship.<br /><br />Mitchell, the Texas Ranger Faith works with, is the brother of Kate Hayden the female main character of <i>The Last Move</i> which was a nice little bonus for those who’ve read that book. Faith and Mitchell’s relationship is already in place when the book starts although it is a physical only one at first. I enjoyed how much these two understood each other plus the physical scenes were very well done. My only issue with the relationship was that it felt like one minute they were no strings and the next they loved each other.<br /><br />As to the plot, the connection between Faith and Macy added a neat layer to the story and I found myself really invested in finding out their history. The parts dealing with the three women found buried at the abandoned ranch was also a really good storyline. This author is amazing at weaving together different plots to create an interesting mystery and this book was no exception. There was the perfect amount of suspense and a solid payoff when it came to the big reveal.<br /><br /><i>Cut and Run</i> was a phenomenal read in terms of the suspense side, I was just hoping for a little more in terms of the romance. Overall though it was an amazing read and I definitely recommend the book if you’re looking for a book with a great suspense plot.<br /><br /><i>**I received an advance copy of this book from Netgalley and the publisher in exchange for an honest review.**</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="6468578499595038697" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2556794451" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2556794451" />
    <a title="♥ WishfulMiss ♥ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/23262703-wishfulmiss"><img alt="♥ WishfulMiss ♥ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1440020691p2/23262703.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2556794451?book_show_action=true">Oct 09, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="♥ WishfulMiss ♥ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="♥ WishfulMiss ♥ " href="/user/show/23262703-wishfulmiss">♥ WishfulMiss ♥ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/23262703-wishfulmiss?shelf=awesome-lady-lead">awesome-lady-lead</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/23262703-wishfulmiss?shelf=law-inforcement-mc">law-inforcement-mc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/23262703-wishfulmiss?shelf=triggers">triggers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/23262703-wishfulmiss?shelf=dark-and-twisty">dark-and-twisty</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/23262703-wishfulmiss?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/23262703-wishfulmiss?shelf=dead-spouse-partner-gf-bf">dead-spouse-partner-gf-bf</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/23262703-wishfulmiss?shelf=romance-fail">romance-fail</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/23262703-wishfulmiss?shelf=mental-physical-abuse">mental-physical-abuse</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/23262703-wishfulmiss?shelf=lacking-romance-little-to-none">lacking-romance-little-to-none</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2556794451" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6257102658737906151"><b>
  <u>Rating: 3.5 Stars</u>
</b><br/><br/>This book was intense! The murder mystery was suspenseful and the author did a really good job of keeping me in the dark about the villain. I didn't have a solid guess until almost the very end, which kept me glued to the book. For the mystery plot this gets a solid 4 stars. I was hooked from beginning to end. The characters all played a part and the more that was revealed, the more I was antsy to get to the conclusion. <br/><br/>What I loved the most has to be the strong female roles</span>
  <span id="freeText6257102658737906151" style="display:none"><b>
  <u>Rating: 3.5 Stars</u>
</b><br /><br />This book was intense! The murder mystery was suspenseful and the author did a really good job of keeping me in the dark about the villain. I didn't have a solid guess until almost the very end, which kept me glued to the book. For the mystery plot this gets a solid 4 stars. I was hooked from beginning to end. The characters all played a part and the more that was revealed, the more I was antsy to get to the conclusion. <br /><br />What I loved the most has to be the strong female roles in this story. Faith, Macy and Kat were strong, capable and fearless. I liked that they each contributed to the story and played a dominant role. <br /><br />I knocked it down half a star because the romance between Faith and Hayden was pretty non-existent. If you completely took the "romance" out, this book would not suffer. Tbh I think it would be better as a strictly mystery/suspense read. The romance was just really cut and dry with them. They were already involved in a purely physical relationship at the start of the story. Then throughout the investigation, the interactions are few and far between and I never felt a real spark of chemistry until the very end. I was surprised how happy I was when both MCs started softening towards the other, but by then it was too little too late for me. <br /><br /><u>A quick summary of the story . . .</u><br />When a body is brought to the morgue, Faith is the pathologist who exams the remains of Jack Crow. He's been tortured, killed and his home ransacked. Texas Ranger Mitchel Hayden is investigating his murder. When Faith reaches out to Crow's daughter, Macy, things get interesting fast. <br /><br />A cold case from 20 years ago is reopened when Crow leaves breadcrumbs for Macy to follow. Her snooping around leads to an attempt on her life. A long lost twin, missing girls, shady adoptions, blackmail and murder lead Faith and Hayden on a twisted path to find the evil master mind behind this new killing spree. <br /><br /><b> <u> Would I recommend?</u></b> Romance wise, this was a bust for me but the mystery part was awesome. Really well done. Highly recommended, but don't expect an epic love story. The romance is scarce.<br /><br /><i><b>* * * ARC provided for an honest review * * *</b><br />I voluntarily read and reviewed an advanced copy of this book. All thoughts and opinions are my own. </i><br /><br /><b>
  <u>SAFETY INFO:</u>
</b> <br /><br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<b><u>Ages</u> </b>: Faith is 30, Hayden is 38. <br /><br /><b><u>Cheating</u> </b> :None. <br /><br /><b><u>OM/OW drama</u> </b> : Technically none. Hayden was married before and his wife died four years ago. Faith knew both while they were married, no mention of their past interactions other than, Faith and wife were "good" friends. I say technically none because we don't really get inside the MCs heads about it and the little that is mentioned is either brushed off or not given any great importance. <br /><br />Personally I didn't enjoy it. Mostly because the little we did get, made it hard for me to buy into Hayden and Faith's love story. <br /><br /> The times she'd seen Hayden and his late wife together made her believe soul mates did in fact exist. <br /><br />Then there was the cold almost clinical sex scenes . . .<br /><br /> The sex had been purely physical. No kissing. No talk of affection. No one was looking for a soul mate. And it suited them both.  <br /><br />I guess for some this isn't too huge a deal breaker since we don't get Faith jealous or hurt by this. Both MCs are just looking for physical relief so no harm, no foul. This was just me personally, not liking that tidbit. It bothered me to know he was obviously capable of tenderness and affection, but the fact that he chooses not to and Faith ends up taking whatever crumbs she can get was not romantic. <br /><br /><blockquote> This was also how it went with them. Neither wanted to look at the other's eyes. She didn't want to see him as a person. And she guessed he was pretending she was the woman he still loved. <br /><br />When things like that are brought up I need closure. I need something concrete from both MCs that they aren't just together for the easily available gratification. I need there to be some emotional connection between them. In the end, it just wasn't convincing to me.<br /><br /><b><u>Separation</u> </b>: None.<br /><br /><b><u>Push/Pull</u></b> : Mutual from both. Again the fact that the romance is not the focal point of this story (I think) helped. It wasn't angsty or emotional. It was factual and mostly stayed on point with the investigation and not their personal relationship.<br /><br /><b><u> Main Pursuer of relationship  </u></b>: Mutual. They both fall into a purely sexual relationship prior to the story even begins. No mention of who made the first move.<br /><br /><b><u>Possible Triggers</u> </b> : Forced captivity, teen pregnancy, adoption, descriptive torture, murder and violence.<br /><br /><b><u>HEA/HFN</u></b> : HFN with a 4 weeks later epilogue.</blockquote> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></span>
  <a data-text-id="6257102658737906151" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10765339-anita?shelf=romantic-supense">romantic-supense</a>,

<span id="freeTextContainer4318987742339410959">Advanced Reader Copy (ARC) provided by the Author and Publisher via NetGalley in exchange for an fair and honest review.<br/><br/>Macy Burton is truly a unique romantic-suspense author. Her plots are never cliché and her heroes and heroines are not what you would expect. She pushes the boundaries and I like that in an author. I sincerely hope that "Cut and Run" is the first in a new series because I love the supporting characters. <br/><br/>Faith McIntyre is the medical examiner and she keeps her life strictly comp</span>
  <span id="freeText4318987742339410959" style="display:none">Advanced Reader Copy (ARC) provided by the Author and Publisher via NetGalley in exchange for an fair and honest review.<br /><br />Macy Burton is truly a unique romantic-suspense author. Her plots are never cliché and her heroes and heroines are not what you would expect. She pushes the boundaries and I like that in an author. I sincerely hope that "Cut and Run" is the first in a new series because I love the supporting characters. <br /><br />Faith McIntyre is the medical examiner and she keeps her life strictly compartmentalized. She has her work, her charity work and her lover and there is very little overlap in those areas. Until. An unconscious woman, a hit and run victim, is found and while she is still alive, Faith is called because this woman has Faith's face. Faith knew she was adopted, she didn't know she was a twin.<br /><br />Macy Crow is an FBI agent. She received a call that her father was brutally murdered and immediately headed to Texas and began her own investigation which landed her clinging to life after a hit and run. When the investigating Texas Ranger, Mitchell Hayden, sees her and sees that Macy is Faith's mirror image, he is relieved that it isn't his lover, Faith, but is at a loss as to what is going on.<br /><br />Texas Ranger Mitchell Hayden lost his wife to cancer and only has the most physical of relationships. His current lover is Faith McIntyre and she is making him think about more than the purely physical. When he starts investigating the brutal murder of Jack Crow he never envisioned where this case would lead. Thirty years is a long time, but secrets have a way of not staying buried, no matter how long the secret has been buried, especially when the secrets have been murdered. Hayden must now solve thirty year old murders and keep both Faith and Macy safe. <b>4 1/2-Stars</b></span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2526572763" />
    <a title="Ann-Marie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/58567012-ann-marie"><img alt="Ann-Marie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594830862p2/58567012.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2526572763?book_show_action=true">Jan 19, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ann-Marie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ann-Marie" href="/user/show/58567012-ann-marie">Ann-Marie</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2526572763" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18387193404625377910">I received this book free in exchange for an honest review.<br/><br/>Mary Burton is an experienced thriller writer. She knows how to develop compelling characters, how to give just enough hints in a plot to be intriguing but not confusing.<br/> But I wonder if the genre itself is running out of steam. It is getting hard for even good writers to come up with a new angle, a story idea that hasn't been done to death, as it were.<br/> All that is left to do is either ratchet up the body count or make the premise unbeli</span>
  <span id="freeText18387193404625377910" style="display:none">I received this book free in exchange for an honest review.<br /><br />Mary Burton is an experienced thriller writer. She knows how to develop compelling characters, how to give just enough hints in a plot to be intriguing but not confusing.<br /> But I wonder if the genre itself is running out of steam. It is getting hard for even good writers to come up with a new angle, a story idea that hasn't been done to death, as it were.<br /> All that is left to do is either ratchet up the body count or make the premise unbelievable, or both.<br /> "Cut and Run" does a little of both. The plot centers around a scheme to impregnate young women, chain them up in a basement until they deliver, kill them and then sell the babies.<br /> If that isn't bad enough, the evildoers start killing each other off years later, along with some innocent bystanders, just to keep the blood flowing.<br /> After dealing with all that, the hero and heroine kiss and ride off into the sunset together. I need months of therapy when I lose a dog to old age. These people must be able to turn off all emotions at will. <br /> The three stars are because there were times I lost myself in the story. That's worth something.</span>
  <a data-text-id="18387193404625377910" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_2557131543" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2557131543" />
    <a title="Trish R." class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/23070724-trish-r"><img alt="Trish R." src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1602800900p2/23070724.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2557131543?book_show_action=true">Oct 13, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Trish R." class="user" itemprop="url" name="Trish R." href="/user/show/23070724-trish-r">Trish R.</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2557131543" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13538181183641571249">So, I’ve read 6 of Mary Burton’s books and I’ve really liked them a lot. BUT this one I loved. Here’s why; the storyline was wonderful but sad, about young girls a man considered “baby makers” then killed the girls after he had the baby, until he had the boy he wanted, but mostly I loved the relationship Hayden (the Texas Ranger) and Faith (the Forensic Pathologist). It went from secret meetings in hotel rooms with no kissing and no facing each other while having sex to a slight peck on the chee</span>
  <span id="freeText13538181183641571249" style="display:none">So, I’ve read 6 of Mary Burton’s books and I’ve really liked them a lot. BUT this one I loved. Here’s why; the storyline was wonderful but sad, about young girls a man considered “baby makers” then killed the girls after he had the baby, until he had the boy he wanted, but mostly I loved the relationship Hayden (the Texas Ranger) and Faith (the Forensic Pathologist). It went from secret meetings in hotel rooms with no kissing and no facing each other while having sex to a slight peck on the cheek to kissing on the lips to falling in love by the end of the book. It was a little romance and sex thrown in with murder and kidnappings to solve. <br /><br />The ONLY problem I had with the story was that Hayden and Faith referred to his dead wife, who died FOUR years ago, as Hayden’s soul-mate and Sierra’s name was mentioned 23 times. I’m not crazy about a dead spouse being mentioned over and over again while the remaining spouse is falling in love again. Mention her 2 or 3 times but NOT 23 times. Just sayin’<br /><br />I liked Macy, the FBI agent who was run down within hours of coming to town and Kat, the teenage girl who was taken by the killer in order to lure Faith to him. It really was exciting from beginning to end.<br /><br />There was graphic sex in this book but certainly NOT erotic. And the F-bomb was used 7 times.<br /><br />As to the narration: The last Mary Burton I read was also narrated by Brittany Pressley and I gave her 2 stars because it was like she didn’t even care if she sounded manly or not so she ruined the book for me. However, this time the men may have all sounded alike but at least the sounded like men. Great job, Ms. Pressley. As of today I will gladly listen to you narrate.<br /><br />This is Mary Burton's newest book and for now it's a free read and free listen. You should grab it up, if you haven't already.</span>
  <a data-text-id="13538181183641571249" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">

<span id="freeTextContainer16367119038841436642">If you are a fan of mysteries and suspense books, then, you need to check out author, Mary Burton. This latest offering from Mary does serve up good characters, a nice storyline with a mix of action and intrigue. <br/><br/>I liked Faith. She was a good mixture of intelligent but personable as well. Thus in turn this made her relatable. A very important quality to have in a character. It makes reading a book much easier. There are several other characters featured in this book. They didn't play second stri</span>
  <span id="freeText16367119038841436642" style="display:none">If you are a fan of mysteries and suspense books, then, you need to check out author, Mary Burton. This latest offering from Mary does serve up good characters, a nice storyline with a mix of action and intrigue. <br /><br />I liked Faith. She was a good mixture of intelligent but personable as well. Thus in turn this made her relatable. A very important quality to have in a character. It makes reading a book much easier. There are several other characters featured in this book. They didn't play second string but equal parts to Faith. <br /><br />Which, I am a fan of this author's and her books. I do have to admit that I struggled in the beginning to really find my footing wit this book. The first chapter or two were good but after that it seemed like there was a lot of time spent in the details of trying to piece everything together. Not that details are not important but too much time spent causes the story to get bogged down. The second half of the book is much better. It is where the most of the action happened. Plus, the story moved faster. There are a few twists along the way. </span>
  <a data-text-id="16367119038841436642" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">

              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1165466571878142082">I read this as my secondary book, just a few pages each day. This wasn't a difficult plot to figure out, but I wasn't expecting it to be. An easy read with characters I liked. I just wish they had been developed a little more in depth.</span>

  <span id="freeText16190109714625257087" style="display:none">Faith is a forensic medical examiner. While investigating a recent find she uncovers evidence that her life, as she knew it, might have been riddled with secrets. A woman laying in a hospital bed, having been the victim of a hit-and-run, could be Faith's twin sister. Just who is Macy Crow, FBI agent, and what does she know that was serious enough to make someone run over her and leave her for dead? Mitchell Hayden, local law enforcement, and Faith have been dating and he's helping her with the investigation. It also makes it possible for him to protect the woman he's falling in love with. <br /><br />Very good book. Lots of intrigue and suspense with just a bit of romance added in. I would definitely recommend this if you're looking for a good book to read on a quiet afternoon. </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer12411158365620154161"><b>3.5 stars</b><br/><br/>Review to follow</span>

<div id="review_3100992134" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3100992134" />
    <a title="Kayla TM" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/100049014-kayla-tm"><img alt="Kayla TM" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1568509131p2/100049014.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3100992134?book_show_action=true">Dec 27, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kayla TM" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kayla TM" href="/user/show/100049014-kayla-tm">Kayla TM</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3100992134" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7573406228430050631">One day, Faith McIntyre is examining the remains of a tortured man named Jim Crow, the next she is at the hospital bedside of Crow’s daughter Macy after she is left clinging to life from a hit-and-run accident. Macy, an FBI agent, has left behind a trail of clues to the mystery surrounding her accident, her father’s death, and the disappearance of a pregnant teenage girl. More than that, Macy has sent Faith a picture of herself: they’re mirror images, adopted twins who had no idea the other exis</span>
  <span id="freeText7573406228430050631" style="display:none">One day, Faith McIntyre is examining the remains of a tortured man named Jim Crow, the next she is at the hospital bedside of Crow’s daughter Macy after she is left clinging to life from a hit-and-run accident. Macy, an FBI agent, has left behind a trail of clues to the mystery surrounding her accident, her father’s death, and the disappearance of a pregnant teenage girl. More than that, Macy has sent Faith a picture of herself: they’re mirror images, adopted twins who had no idea the other existed. With twists and turns, and a bit of romance sprinkled in, Faith and Texas Ranger Mitchell Hayden make a series of discoveries that have them digging into three disappearances from thirty years earlier that have Faith questioning everything she knew about her past.<br /><br />Although it has claims of being a romance, the actual romance is more erotic. The remainder of the romantic relationship seems to have built before the book’s opening, and while there are small moments where they seem to be moving forward, it feels like the relationship suddenly happened rather than built. It is not a main theme of the story, though it pretends to be. The thriller portion of the novel, is great. Intriguing, with a whodunnit nature that, while I had it figured out, does keep the reader guessing. The ending, however, I found to be lacking. Yes, it wraps up and answers a great many questions, but there was more I wanted from it. I don’t feel like everything was taken care of. I want to know about other people’s involvement. How everything came to be, and that just isn’t covered to the extent I would like. Still a good book though. I’m rounding up to four stars even though it feels like it’s between a three and a four. </span>
  <a data-text-id="7573406228430050631" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2697880449" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2697880449" />
    <a title="Lily (Night Owl Book Cafe)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12907755-lily-night-owl-book-cafe"><img alt="Lily (Night Owl Book Cafe)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1347992956p2/12907755.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2697880449?book_show_action=true">Mar 01, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lily (Night Owl Book Cafe)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lily (Night Owl Book Cafe)" href="/user/show/12907755-lily-night-owl-book-cafe">Lily (Night Owl Book Cafe)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2697880449" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7982041448345033112">First time dipping my toes into Mary Burton's world and it won't be my last!<br/><br/>Cut and Run follows a medical examiner Faith McIntyre, who finds that the woman lies in critical condition is her twin sister she never knew about. Faith always knew she was adopted, but she didn't know that her adoption would unearth a trail of deep dark secrets. Following the clues her twin left behind, Faith and Texas Ranger Mitchell Hayden will uncover shocking discoveries of the past that might help them find a new </span>
  <span id="freeText7982041448345033112" style="display:none">First time dipping my toes into Mary Burton's world and it won't be my last!<br /><br />Cut and Run follows a medical examiner Faith McIntyre, who finds that the woman lies in critical condition is her twin sister she never knew about. Faith always knew she was adopted, but she didn't know that her adoption would unearth a trail of deep dark secrets. Following the clues her twin left behind, Faith and Texas Ranger Mitchell Hayden will uncover shocking discoveries of the past that might help them find a new missing pregnant girl in the present.<br /><br />This book was a really good thriller. Well written, with great character development. I loved that Faith and Mitchell weren't exactly perfect, which made them easy to relate to and more human.<br /><br />I love the dark atmospheric tone of the book. I really enjoyed the pace. The overall story kept me mostly guessing and gave me enough to make me want to flip through the pages. The themes were a bit dark and as a mother, hard to read at times. But overall the well-developed plot was exciting and heart pounding till the end. I liked that the authors sprinkled a little bit of romance to lighten the plot line.<br /><br />I think my only gripe with all of this would be the ending. I thought it felt a bit rushed as everything fell into place and the last bit was uncovered. I would have liked the reveal to unravel a bit slower.<br /><br />But I really enjoyed her style of writing and storytelling, I will be looking for more from this author.<a href="https://nightowlbookcafe.com/2019/03/01/review-cut-and-run-by-mary-burton/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">This review was originally posted on Night Owl Book Cafe</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="7982041448345033112" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2509944479" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2509944479" />
    <a title="RachelW (BamaGal)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/31722634-rachelw-bamagal"><img alt="RachelW (BamaGal)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1467470328p2/31722634.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2509944479?book_show_action=true">Sep 23, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="RachelW (BamaGal)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="RachelW (BamaGal)" href="/user/show/31722634-rachelw-bamagal">RachelW (BamaGal)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2509944479" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12205024273882415696">Another good RS read by Mary Burton; an author who I’ve come to quite enjoy reading. The long-lost twin sister trope almost made me groan out loud; but Burton tossed all the old cliches out and came up with a rather original idea for the plotline. The book wasn’t actually about the two sisters working together, though; as one of the twins was in the hospital for most of the book. <br/><br/>There was still a bit of the usual clunky ending for a Burton book; the big villain ‘this is what I did and why I did</span>
  <span id="freeText12205024273882415696" style="display:none">Another good RS read by Mary Burton; an author who I’ve come to quite enjoy reading. The long-lost twin sister trope almost made me groan out loud; but Burton tossed all the old cliches out and came up with a rather original idea for the plotline. The book wasn’t actually about the two sisters working together, though; as one of the twins was in the hospital for most of the book. <br /><br />There was still a bit of the usual clunky ending for a Burton book; the big villain ‘this is what I did and why I did it’ tell all. Burton really needs to work on that; but otherwise this was a well done RS story. The big bad killing off the lesser big bads one by one was a nice touch, if a bit gory. I’m looking forward to more reads in this series. The mixup of FBI and the Texas Rangers sounds promising.</span>
  <a data-text-id="12205024273882415696" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('TmC+eZWPtH+zC0vYO2Wonmw9IEotIt3cY2o5uH/g9Fp65MtMXX2qwo9+MUriS+ImOGOrI7HXYJz3JOnCPREecg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('RtM/eN1Ek7+GIoThci8ERWwjKq5iHgO1IpbLnNBzFJ9yV0pNFbaNArpX/nOrAU79OH2hx/7rvvW22BvmkoL+tw==')})
  }

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer888902639640549766"><br/><br/><br/>Mary Burton, whose latest novel is Hide and Seek, loves writing suspense, getting to know her characters, keeping up with law enforcement and forensic procedure, morning walks, baking, and tiny dachshunds. She also enjoys hunting down serial killers, which she does in her New York Times and USA Today bestselling novels. Library Journal has compared her work to that of Lisa Jackson and Lisa Gardner</span>
  <span id="freeText888902639640549766" style="display:none"><br /><br /><br />Mary Burton, whose latest novel is Hide and Seek, loves writing suspense, getting to know her characters, keeping up with law enforcement and forensic procedure, morning walks, baking, and tiny dachshunds. She also enjoys hunting down serial killers, which she does in her New York Times and USA Today bestselling novels. Library Journal has compared her work to that of Lisa Jackson and Lisa Gardner, and Fresh Fiction likened her writing to that of James Patterson.<br /><br />Mary is routinely featured among the top ten writers in Amazon’s Author Rankings for romantic suspense. Upon publication, her novels, including 2018’s Cut and Run and Her Last Word, consistently rank high on the Kindle eBooks Store Bestseller List. <br /><br />Additionally, Cut and Run has been nominated for the Romance Writers of America’s prestigious RITA Award for Romantic Suspense. Previous recipients in this category include Nora Roberts, J.D. Robb, Tess Gerritsen, Karen Rose and Mary Jo Putney. The award will be announced at the RITA Award Ceremony July 26th in New York City during the organization’s annual conference. <br /><br />A Richmond native, Mary has lived there for most of her life. Her first book was published in 2000. Her first book was published in 2000. Today she’s the author of thirty-two published novels and five novellas as Mary Burton and five works of contemporary fiction written as Mary Ellen Taylor, including 2018’s Winter Cottage. She is co-editor with novelist Mary Miley of Deadly Southern Charm, A Lethal Ladies Mystery Anthology.<br /><br />A member of International Thriller Writers, Sisters in Crime, Mystery Writers of America, Novelists, Inc., and Romance Writers of America, Mary is known for creating multiple suspense stories connected by characters and/or place.<br /></span>
